    <aside id="interscroller_ad" class="interscroller_ad visible-xs center mobile-interscroller " style="width:300px"></aside>
    <script>
        var mps = mps || {};
        mps._queue = mps._queue || {};
        mps._queue.gptloaded = mps._queue.gptloaded || [];
        mps._queue.adload = mps._queue.adload || [];

        mps._queue.gptloaded.push(function() {
            if (mps.getResponsiveSet() =='0') { //MOBILE
                mps.insertAd('#interscroller_ad','interscroller');
            }
        });
        mps._queue.adload.push(function(eo) {
            if (eo._mps._slot === 'interscroller' && eo.isEmpty) {
                document.querySelector('.mobile-interscroller').classList.add('isEmpty');
            }
        });
    </script>

<section id="audience_reviews" class="panel panel-rt panel-box" data-qa="audience-reviews">
    <h2 class="panel-heading">Audience Reviews for <em>Ralph Breaks the Internet</em></h2>
    
        
        <div class="sr-only js-clamp-live-region" aria-live="polite"></div>
        <ul class="mop-audience-reviews__reviews-wrap clearfix">
            
            
            
                <li class="mop-audience-reviews__review-item pull-left cl" data-qa="quote-bubble">
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review-quote" data-qa="quote-bubble-review">
                        <div class=" clearfix">
                            
                                <span class="star-display" data-qa="star-display"><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__empty"></span></span>
                            
                            <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--duration">Aug 08, 2019</span>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--comment clamp clamp-4 js-clamp">It&#39;s Disney doing the Emoji Movie.  That&#39;s really what this is when it comes down to it.  And honestly…it&#39;s not bad.  I mean yeah it&#39;s still riddled with product placement and an egregious amount of Disney marketing, but it&#39;s still charming and funny enough that it kinda&#39; works.  While we&#39;ve seen other movies and TV shows tackle this &quot;internet as a city&quot; concept before, seeing it with Disney talent is actually pretty cool.  I liked eBay as a store, I liked pop up ads as annoying guys on the street, hell as ridiculously filtered as it was I even kinda&#39; liked how they showed the Dark Web!  Seriously, the Dark Web in a Disney movie!  I mean they Nerfed the hell out of it but still, pretty crazy.  However I do miss the video game elements that were such a big part of the original film, that really feel missing here.  One of my favorite parts of this film is the online game Slaughter Race, and it&#39;s really cool to see how they handle online gaming, and handle a game that&#39;s basically Twisted Metal through a Disney filter which is pretty fun.  However, it&#39;s just one game.  I also found the handling of Ralph&#39;s character really clumsy here.  He made mistakes in the first movie, but he had a good heart.  Here, he makes some choices that make it really hard to root for him.  Yeah he learns his lesson, but it makes his development in the original feel forgotten and he comes off really selfish.  In the end it&#39;s a flawed but still really fun movie.</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-wrap">
                        
                            <a href="/user/id/901376268">
                            
                                <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-default"></span>
                            
                            </a>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name-wrap">
                            
                                <a href="/user/id/901376268">
                                    <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name">Michael M</span>
                                </a>
                            
                            
                                <strong class="super-reviewer-badge">Super Reviewer</strong>
                            
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </li>
                
                <li class="mop-audience-reviews__review-item pull-right cr" data-qa="quote-bubble">
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review-quote" data-qa="quote-bubble-review">
                        <div class=" clearfix">
                            
                                <span class="star-display" data-qa="star-display"><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__half "></span><span class="star-display__empty"></span></span>
                            
                            <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--duration">Mar 14, 2019</span>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--comment clamp clamp-4 js-clamp">There isn&#39;t a central bad guy here and I felt it robbed the film. The first film failed to deliver a true scary villain and played out like a Marvel film that focuses on the hero, even if he is flawed. This sequel is about the same quality for my liking and it delivers a lot of heart, but not a lot of substance. I don&#39;t know where the franchise can go from here and this film balances a tight rope of becoming a series that drops in quality with each film. There was something lacking with the film overall and I felt they attempted too much. Visually it&#39;s stunning and I tip my cap to the filmmakers on this. I think they could have played with the pop culture more, and that was my issue with the first film. I could not say this was better or worse, but as a continuation it elevates the heart of the franchise. 14/03/2019</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-wrap">
                        
                            <a href="/user/id/909990449">
                            
                                <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-default"></span>
                            
                            </a>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name-wrap">
                            
                                <a href="/user/id/909990449">
                                    <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--name">Brendan N</span>
                                </a>
                            
                            
                                <strong class="super-reviewer-badge">Super Reviewer</strong>
                            
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </li>
                
                <li class="mop-audience-reviews__review-item pull-left cl" data-qa="quote-bubble">
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review-quote" data-qa="quote-bubble-review">
                        <div class=" clearfix">
                            
                                <span class="star-display" data-qa="star-display"><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__half "></span><span class="star-display__empty"></span></span>
                            
                            <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--duration">Mar 01, 2019</span>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--comment clamp clamp-4 js-clamp">As a proud product of 2018, it is safe to say that this movie will soon be dated and half of its jokes will be lost for a new generation, but despite that (and the fact that the climax is a bit messy), it can be quite entertaining with its concept and design of an internet world.</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-wrap">
                        
                            <a href="/user/id/891372896">
                            
                                <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--user-default"></span>

                    <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review-quote" data-qa="quote-bubble-review">
                        <div class=" clearfix">
                            
                                <span class="star-display" data-qa="star-display"><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__filled "></span><span class="star-display__empty"></span></span>
                            
                            <span class="mop-audience-reviews__review--duration">Feb 18, 2019</span>
                        </div>
                        
                        <div class="mop-audience-reviews__review--comment clamp clamp-4 js-clamp">A sequel that surpasses the original, with a sweet story that is steeped in creativity and truly proves the animators at Disney have imagination galore. Well written and acted and Reily is winning again as Ralph. Very Funny to boot.! 02-17-2019</div>
